  pencilscroller();
  var counter = 0;

  /*
   * Pencil Carousel
   */
  function pencilscroller() {
    if (document.getElementById('fixedpencil-subs')) {
      carousel();
    } else if (counter <= 10) {
      setTimeout(pencilscroller, 10000);
      counter++;
    }
  }

  var slideIndex_pen = 0;

  function carousel() {
    slideIndex_pen = slideIndex_pen ? slideIndex_pen : 0;
    var i;
    var x = document.getElementsByClassName("subs_valueprop");
    for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
      x[i].style.display = "none";
    }
    slideIndex_pen++;
    if (slideIndex_pen > x.length) {
      slideIndex_pen = 1;
    }
    x[slideIndex_pen - 1].style.display = "block";
    setTimeout(carousel, 2500);
  }

  /*
   * Check browser is IE
   */
  const notIE = !(window.navigator.userAgent.indexOf("MSIE ") > 0 || !!navigator.userAgent.match(/Trident.*rv\:11\./));

  /*
   * Get Cookie - to read any cookie
   */
  function getCookie(cname) {
    var name = cname + "=";
    var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
    var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
    for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
      var c = ca[i];
      while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
        c = c.substring(1);
      }
      if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
        return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  /*
   * Hide Subscription Pencil
   */
  function hidearcpencil() {
    var styleNode = document.createElement("style");
    var styleText = document.createTextNode("#subscription-pencil-area { display:none  !important; }");
    styleNode.setAttribute("id", "hidepencil");
    styleNode.type = "text/css";
    styleNode.appendChild(styleText);
    document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(styleNode);
  }

  /*

  /*
   * Returns whether or not localStorage is supported/settable in current browser
   * @returns {Boolean}
   */
  function localStorageIsSupported() {
    const testKey = "test";
    const localStorageExists = "localStorage" in window;

    if (!localStorageExists) { // localStorage is not a property of window
      return false;
    }

    try {
      window.localStorage.setItem(testKey, "1");
      window.localStorage.removeItem(testKey);
      console.log("[Darwin bg] Local storage is supported");
      return true;
    } catch (error) {
      // Local storage does not exist or is full.
      console.log("[Darwin bg] Local storage is unsupported");
      return false;
    }
  }

  /*
   * Detect if the browser is running in Private Browsing mode
   * @export
   * @returns {Promise}
   */
  function isPrivateMode() {
    return new Promise(function (resolve) {
      const on = function () {
        return resolve(true);
      } // is in private mode
      const off = function () {
        return resolve(false);
      } // not private mode
      const testLocalStorage = function () {
        try {
          if (localStorage.length) off();
          else {
            localStorage.x = 1;
            localStorage.removeItem('x');
            off();
          }
        } catch (e) {
          // Safari only enables cookie in private mode
          // if cookie is disabled then all client side storage is disabled
          // if all client side storage is disabled, then there is no point
          // in using private mode
          navigator.cookieEnabled ? on() : off();
        }
      };
      // Chrome & Opera
      if (window.webkitRequestFileSystem) {
        return void window.webkitRequestFileSystem(0, 0, off, on);
      }
      // Firefox
      if ('MozAppearance' in document.documentElement.style) {
        const db = indexedDB.open('test');
        db.onerror = on;
        db.onsuccess = off;
        return void 0;
      }
      // Safari
      const isSafari = navigator.userAgent.match(/Version\/([0-9\._]+).*Safari/);
      if (isSafari) {
        const version = parseInt(isSafari[1], 10);
        if (version >= 11) {
          try {
            var dbname = "hasDB";
            window.openDatabase(dbname, "1.0", dbname, 0);
            return off();
          } catch (_) {
            return on();
          };
        } else if (version < 11) {
          return testLocalStorage();
        }
      }
      // if (/constructor/i.test(window.HTMLElement)) {
      //   return testLocalStorage();
      // }

      // IE10+ & Edge
      if (!window.indexedDB && (window.PointerEvent || window.MSPointerEvent)) {
        return on();
      }
      // others
      return off();
    });
  }

  const supportsLocalStorage = localStorageIsSupported();

  function isAdBlocked() {

    var isadblock = adElement ? !(adElement.offsetWidth || adElement.offsetHeight || adElement.getClientRects()
      .length) : true;
    return isadblock;
  }

  /*
   * Call any api to get the corresponding results

   */
  function getapi(url, compare) {
    if (window.navigator.userAgent.indexOf("MSIE ") === -1) {
      return fetch(url)
        .then(function (resp) {
          return resp.json();
        })
        .then(function (data) {
          //cem1515
          if (compare.test === '1515') {
            return {
              data
            }
          }

          //cem1706
          if (compare.test === '1706') {
            return {
              data
            }
          }

        })
        .catch(function (error) {
          console.err('fetch error: ', error)
          return error;
        });
    } else {
      return false;
    }
  }

  /*
   * Call graphiql to get the corresponding results
   * @returns {Object}
   */
  function getapi_graphiql(url, compare) {
    if (window.navigator.userAgent.indexOf("MSIE ") === -1) {
      return fetch(url, {
          method: "POST",
          body: compare[0]
        })
        .then(function (resp) {
          return resp.json();
        })
        .then(function (data) {
          var output = [];
          output[0] = compare[1];
          output[1] = data;
          document.cookie = "getloginsessions_api= " + JSON.stringify(output) + ";" + "expires=" + new Date(new Date()
            .getTime() + 60 * 60 * 1000 * 24).toGMTString() + ";path=/";
          return getArticle(data);
        })
        .catch(function (error) {
          return error;
        });
    } else {
      return false;
    }
  }

  /*
   * Call to flatten the results from api
   * @returns {Object}
   */
  function flattenObj(data) {
    var result = {};

    function recurse(cur, prop) {
      if (Object(cur) !== cur) {
        result[prop] = cur;
      } else if (Array.isArray(cur)) {
        for (var i = 0, l = cur.length; i < l; i++)
          recurse(cur[i], prop + "[" + i + "]");
        if (l == 0)
          result[prop] = [];
      } else {
        var isEmpty = true;
        for (var p in cur) {
          isEmpty = false;
          recurse(cur[p], prop ? prop + "." + p : p);
        }
        if (isEmpty && prop)
          result[prop] = {};
      }
    }
    recurse(data, "");
    return result;
  }

  /*
   * Push Analytics
   * testId = test name eg: cem###
   * feature = element name eg: paywall, pencil
   * action = type of action eg: display, clickCTA
   * label = label name of element eg: SubscribeNow
   * variant = name of variant eg: control, experience
   * segment = name of segment eg: anony, subs
   */
  function pushAnalytics(testId, feature, action, label, variant, segment) {
    analyticsLayer.push({
      "event": "clickEvent",
      "clickEvent": {
        "testId": testId,
        "feature": feature || '',
        "action": action || '',
        "type": "test",
        "label": label || '',
        "variantName": variant,
        "segmentName": segment
      }
    });
  }

           <div class="c-card gi-covid-widget">
            <div class="virus-widget-section virus-widget-section_meta">
             <span class="tag">
              COVID-19 by the numbers
             </span>
            </div>
           </div>
           <script>
            (function covidWeekly() {
    function numFormat(num) {
      return new Intl.NumberFormat("en-US").format(Number(num));
    }
    function handleJSON(response) {
      return response.json();
    }
    function changeDirection(val) {
      var res = "no-change";
      if (val.charAt(0) == "-") {
        res = "down";
      } else if (Number(val.split("%")[0]) > 0) {
        res = "up";
      }
      return res;
    }
    function initWidget(urls) {
      Promise.all(
        urls.map(function item(url) {
          return fetch(url).then(handleJSON);
        })
      ).then(updateCoronavirusNumbersWidget);
    }
    function updateCoronavirusNumbersWidget(data) {
      var summary = data[0];
      var weekly = data[1];
      var bcData = weekly.elements[0]; // only province with period
      var natData = weekly.elements[weekly.elements.length - 1]; // Canada
      var element = document.querySelector(".gi-covid-widget");
      element.innerHTML = [
        '<div class="virus-widget-section virus-widget-section_meta">',
          '<span class="tag">COVID-19 by the numbers</span>',
          '<span class="timestamp">As of ' + summary.updated + '</span>',
        '</div>',
        '<div class="virus-widget-group">',
        '<div class="virus-widget-section virus-section">',
          '<div class="header-row">',
            '<span>&nbsp;</span>',
            '<span>Total reported</span>',
            '<span>' + bcData["period"]+ '</span>',
            '<span>7-day change</span>',
          '</div>',
          '<div class="val-row">',
            '<span class="row-header">Cases</span>',
            '<span>' + numFormat(natData.cases) + '</span>',
            '<span>' + numFormat(natData.caseslastday) + '</span>',
            '<span class="change ' + changeDirection(natData["cases-weekly-change"]) + '">' + natData["cases-weekly-change"] + '</span>',
          '</div>',
          '<div class="val-row">',
            '<span class="row-header">Deaths</span>',
            '<span>' + numFormat(natData.deaths) + '</span>',
            '<span>' + numFormat(natData.deathslastday) + '</span>',
            '<span class="change ' + changeDirection(natData["deaths-weekly-change"]) + '">' + natData["deaths-weekly-change"] + '</span>',
          '</div>',
          '<div class="val-row">',
            '<span class="row-header">Hospitalized</span>',
            '<span>&nbsp;</span>',
            '<span>' + numFormat(natData.hospitals) + '</span>',
            '<span class="change ' + changeDirection(natData["hospitals-change"]) + '">' + natData["hospitals-change"] + '</span>',
          '</div>',
        '</div>',
        '<div class="virus-widget-section vaccination-section">',
          '<div class="vaccination-section-header"><span class="row-header">Vaccinations</span></div>',
          '<div class="header-row">',
            '<span>Doses <span class="gi-break"></span>administered</span>',
            '<span>Doses per <span class="gi-break"></span>100 people</span>',
          '</div>',
          '<div class="val-row">',
            '<span>'+ numFormat(natData["dosesadmin"]) + ' <span class="change">(' + natData["dosesadmin-pct"] + '  of doses distributed)</span></span>',
            '<span>'+ Number((natData["dosesadmin"] / natData["population"]) * 100).toFixed(1) + '</span>',
          '</div>',
        '</div>',
        '<div class="virus-widget-section links-section">',
          '<div class="coronavirusinfo--links">',
            '<ul class="coronavirusinfo__links u-clearfix">',
              '<li>',
                '<a href="/world/article-coronavirus-covid19-latest-news-canada-explainer/" data-analyticsclick=\'{"feature":"coronavirusinfo","type":"link","label":"live updates coronavirus guide","position":1,"hierarchy":2}\'>Live updates: what you need to know</a>',
              '</li>',
              '<li>',
                '<a href="/newsletters/?utm_source=onsite&utm_medium=coronavirusinfo&utm_campaign=Corona_mkt&utm_term=newsletter&utm_content=corona#coronavirus-update" data-analyticsclick=\'{"feature":"coronavirusinfo","type":"link","label":"sign up daily newsletter","position":1,"hierarchy":2}\'>Sign up: coronavirus newsletter</a>',
              '</li>',
              '<li>',
                '<a href="/canada/article-covid-19-vaccine-rollout-in-canada-by-province-explainer/" data-analyticsclick=\'{"feature":"coronavirusinfo","type":"link","label":"our guide to the vaccine rollout","position":1,"hierarchy":2}\'>Our guide to the vaccine rollout</a>',
              '</li>',
              '<li>',
                '<a href="politics/article-canada-covid-19-travel-restrictions-quarantine-hotel-testing-explainer/" data-analyticsclick=\'{"feature":"coronavirusinfo","type":"link","label":"the new rules for travellers","position":1,"hierarchy":2}\'>The new rules for travellers</a>',
              '</li>',
            '</ul>',
          '</div>',
        '</div>',
        '<span class="row-header">Explore in depth:</span>',
        '<div class="virus-widget-section cta-section">' ,
          '<a class="gi-covid-widget_cta" href="/canada/article-coronavirus-cases-canada-world-map-explainer/">latest numbers and trends</a> | <a class="gi-covid-widget_cta" href="/canada/article-covid-19-vaccine-tracker-canada-latest-numbers-explainer/">track the vaccine rollout</a>',
        '</div>',
      ].join("");
    }
    try {
      var endpoints = [
        "https://covid-19-2020-prod-dc5q4g5x5w7l.s3.ca-central-1.amazonaws.com/summary.json",
        "https://covid-19-2020-prod-dc5q4g5x5w7l.s3.ca-central-1.amazonaws.com/weekly-change.json",
      ];
      initWidget(endpoints);
    } catch (e) {
      console.error("covid-weekly feature", e);
    }
  })();
           </script>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>

                  This is the Power Gap: Explore the investigative series and data
                 </div>
                </div>
                <div class="c-card__dek">
                 The first equal pay legislation in Canada passed in 1951, making it illegal to pay men and women in the same job different salaries. Women overtook men among university graduates three decades ago. Today, women represent just under half of the workforce. And yet, men still dramatically outnumber, outrank and outearn women.

             <div class="c-card">
              <a class="c-card__grid c-card__link" data-analyticsclick='{"type":"link","feature":"video","contentId":"1a6ffadd-3493-47ef-8cee-a39faf7424f9","label":"explorer dives to the deepest point on earth","page":"sec:homepage:video","hierarchy":1}' data-lt-lid="Headline." data-lt-pos="sec:homepage:video" data-sophi="1a6ffadd-3493-47ef-8cee-a39faf7424f9" href="/world/video-explorer-dives-to-the-deepest-point-on-earth/">
               <div class="c-card__content">
                <div class="c-card__hed">
                 <div class="c-card__hed-text">
                  Explorer dives to the deepest point on Earth
                 </div>
                 <span aria-label="Video" class="c-indicator-icon c-indicator-icon--video">
                  <svg aria-hidden="true" class="c-indicator-icon__art c-indicator-icon__art--video" focusable="false" pointer-events="none" role="img">
                   <use xlink:href="/pb/resources/assets/panther/sprites/sprite.bb2f3a4bd66b1c1009c7d47970a85730.svg#icon-video">
                   </use>
                  </svg>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="c-card__dek">
                 Space and sea explorer and noted computer game developer Richard Garriott is the first person in the world to have explored the North Pole, the South Pole, flown to the International Space Station and descended to the deepest point on Earth - the Mariana Trench.
                </div>
               </div>

          var variantData = data;
          /**
 * *************** HELPER FUNCTIONS ********************
 */
// Get one element
function qs(selectors, baseElement) {
  var base = baseElement || window.document;
  return base.querySelector(selectors);
}

// Get an array of elements.
function qsa(selectors, baseElement) {
  var base = baseElement || window.document;
  return [].slice.call(base.querySelectorAll(selectors));
}

/**
 * Get the test group for the user
 * @returns {String|undefined}
 */
function userTestGroup() {
  if (variant.is("control")) {
    return "control";
  }
  if (variant.is("variant")) {
    return "variant";
  }
}

/**
 * Get the user guid
 * @returns {String|undefined}
 */
function getUserGuid() {
  return window.tgam &&
    window.tgam.datalayer &&
    window.tgam.datalayer.identity &&
    window.tgam.datalayer.identity.guid;
}

// Get the environment
function getEnv() {
  var isProdOrStage = window.tgam.env.isProdOrStage;
  var env = isProdOrStage === true ? "prd" : "dev";
  return env;
}

/**
 * ************ FUNCTIONS TO CONSTRUCT THE STORY CARD IN LATEST FEED *****************
 */
/**
 * Get the label data if exists
 * @param {Object} article - that contains label
 * @returns {Object} of label
 */
function getLabel(article) {
  var labelText = "";
  if (article.section_label && article.section_label !== "") {
    labelText = article.section_label.toLowerCase();
  }
  if (
    article.label &&
    article.label.basic &&
    article.label.basic.display === true &&
    article.label.basic.text &&
    labelText == ""
  ) {
    labelText = article.label.basic.text.toLowerCase();
  }
  return labelText;
}

/**
 * Get all the data to display the image
 * @param {Object} article - that contains image
 * @param {String} label - story label
 * @returns {Object} of image
 */
function getImage(article, label) {
  var path = null;
  var alt = null;
  var isOpinion = label.text === "opinion" || article.subtype === "column";

  // Show author image if opinion/column article
  if (isOpinion) {
    if (
      article.authors &&
      article.authors.length &&
      article.authors[0].metadata &&
      article.authors[0].metadata.image
    ) {
      // This image is preferred because it has been resized
      path = article.authors[0].metadata.image;
      alt = article.authors[0].byline;
    } else if (
      article.credits &&
      article.credits.by &&
      article.credits.by.length &&
      article.credits.by[0].image &&
      article.credits.by[0].image.url
    ) {
      path = article.credits.by[0].image.url;
      alt = article.credits.by[0].name;
    }
    if (path) {
      return { path: path, alt: alt };
    } else {
      path = null;
    }
  }
  // Article image
  alt =
    article.promo_items &&
    article.promo_items.basic &&
    article.promo_items.basic.caption
      ? article.promo_items.basic.caption
      : "";

  if (
    article.pictureRel &&
    article.pictureRel.length &&
    article.pictureRel[0].url200
  ) {
    // This image is preferred because it has been resized
    path = article.pictureRel[0].url200;
    if (!alt) {
      alt = article.pictureRel[0].caption;
    }
  } else if (
    article.promo_items &&
    article.promo_items.basic &&
    article.promo_items.basic.url
  ) {
    path = article.promo_items.basic.url;
  }
  if (path) {
    return { path: path, alt: alt };
  }
  return { path: null, alt: null };
}

/**
 * Generate a template for the time. Based on PB dateDisplay.tag Note that `js-moment` stuff has not
 * been copied over, but we still add a class below. A future enhancement would be to complete
 * implementing this feature. I don't think it's worth it at this point, just for Darwin tests.
 * @param {Object} article - to process
 * @returns {String}
 */
function displayDateTag(article) {
  var isSectionPageContext = ["story", "video"].indexOf(window.tgam.meta.pagetype) === -1;
  var storyPublishedDate = storyPublishedDateTag(article);

  if (!storyPublishedDate || !window.Intl || !window.Intl.DateTimeFormat) {
    return "";
  }

  var storyDate = storyTimeDisplayTag({
    pubdate: storyPublishedDate,
    update: article.last_updated_date,
    isSectionPageContext: isSectionPageContext
  });

  var publishedDate = storyDate.published; // Month D, YYYY
  var updatedDate = storyDate.updated;
  var hideUpdate = storyDate.field === "published";
  var publishedPreface = isSectionPageContext ? "" : "Published ";
  var updatedPreface = "Updated" + (isSectionPageContext ? "" : " ");
  var publishedClassNames = storyDate.moment === "published" || storyDate.moment === "both" ? " jx-story-moment" : "";
  var updatedClassNames = (storyDate.moment === "updated" || storyDate.moment === "both" ? " jx-story-moment" : "") + (hideUpdate ? " u-visually-hidden" : "");
  updatedClassNames = updatedClassNames + (isSectionPageContext ? " c-timestamp--updated" : "");

  // "Time ago" timestamp
  var date = since(storyPublishedDate);
  if (date === "") {
    // If "time ago" is empty (means article is older than three days) display the date
    date = publishedDate;
  }

  return [
    "<time class='c-card__meta-time u-no-wrap ", publishedClassNames, "'>", publishedPreface, date, "</time>",
    " ", // keep space for layout
    "<time class='c-card__meta-time u-no-wrap ", updatedClassNames, "'>", updatedPreface, (isSectionPageContext ? "" : updatedDate), "</time>"
  ].join("");
}

// Based on PB storyTimeDisplay.tag
function storyPublishedDateTag(story) {
  return story.display_date || story.publish_date;
}

// Based on PB storyTimeDisplay.tag
function storyTimeDisplayTag(params) {
  var isSectionPageContext = true;
  var pubDate = new Date(params.pubdate);
  var upDate = new Date(params.update);
  var now = new Date();

  var oneYear = 31536000;
  var oneDay = 86400;
  var threeDays = 259200;
  var tenMinutes = 600;
  var unixNow = Math.round(now.getTime() / 1000);
  var unixPubdate = Math.round(pubDate.getTime() / 1000);
  var unixUpdate = Math.round(upDate.getTime() / 1000);
  var timeSincePublication = unixNow - unixPubdate;
  var timeSinceUpdate = unixNow - unixUpdate;

  var pattern = {
    year: "numeric",
    month: "long",
    day: "numeric",
    timeZone: "America/Toronto"
  };

  if (params.format) {
    pattern = params.format;
  } else if (isSectionPageContext && timeSincePublication < oneYear) {
    pattern = {
      month: "long",
      day: "numeric",
      timeZone: "America/Toronto"
    };
  }

  // https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/DateTimeFormat
  var formatter = new Intl.DateTimeFormat("en-US", pattern);

  var formattedPubDate = formatter.format(pubDate);
  var formattedUpDate = formatter.format(upDate);

  var publishedAndUpdatedAreTheSameDay = formattedPubDate === formattedUpDate;
  var publishedLessThanThreeDaysAgo = timeSincePublication < threeDays;
  var updatedWasLessThanThreeDaysAgo = timeSinceUpdate < threeDays;
  var storyWasUnderEmbargoOrSimilar = unixPubdate > unixUpdate;
  var storyHasBeenUpdatedMoreThanTenMinutesSincePublication = !storyWasUnderEmbargoOrSimilar && ((unixUpdate - unixPubdate) > tenMinutes);
  var showPublishedDateAsMoment = publishedLessThanThreeDaysAgo;
  var showUpdatedDateAsMoment = !isSectionPageContext && storyHasBeenUpdatedMoreThanTenMinutesSincePublication && updatedWasLessThanThreeDaysAgo;

  var field = "published"; // Which fields to show (published, updated, or both)
  var moment = null; // Which fields to show in relative date (i.e., moment) format

  if (storyHasBeenUpdatedMoreThanTenMinutesSincePublication) {
    if (publishedAndUpdatedAreTheSameDay && timeSinceUpdate < oneDay) {
      field = "both"; // Don't show updated date since it's the same as published date.
    }
  }

  if (showUpdatedDateAsMoment) {
    moment = "updated";

    if (showPublishedDateAsMoment) {
      moment = "both";
    }

  } else if (showPublishedDateAsMoment) {
    moment = "published";
  }

  return {
    published: formattedPubDate,
    updated: formattedUpDate,
    field: field,
    moment: moment
  };
}

// Show "time ago" timestamp
function humanTime(left, right) {
  var amount = parseInt(right - left).toFixed(0);
  var ONE_MINUTE = 60;
  var ONE_HOUR = 3600;
  var ONE_DAY = 86400;
  var THREE_DAYS = 259200;
  var plural;

  if (amount < ONE_MINUTE) {
    plural = amount === 1 ? "" : "s";
    return amount + " second" + plural + " ago";
  }
  if (amount < ONE_HOUR) {
    amount = Math.round(amount / ONE_MINUTE);
    plural = amount === 1 ? "" : "s";
    return amount + " minute" + plural + " ago";
  }
  if (amount >= ONE_HOUR && amount < ONE_DAY) {
    amount = Math.round(amount / ONE_HOUR);
    plural = amount === 1 ? "" : "s";
    return amount + " hour" + plural + " ago";
  }
  if (amount >= ONE_DAY && amount < THREE_DAYS) {
    amount = Math.round(amount / ONE_DAY);
    plural = amount === 1 ? "" : "s";
    return amount + " day" + plural + " ago";
  }
  return "";
}

// Calculate time since published
function since(storyDate) {
  var left = new Date(storyDate).getTime() / 1000;
  var right = Date.now() / 1000;
  return humanTime(left, right);
}

//********** TEMPLATES FOR DIFFERENT CARD ELEMENTS *********
/**
 * Generates image template
 * @param {Object} image - to render
 * @returns {String}
 */
function displayImage(image) {
  var template = "";
  if (image.path) {
    template = [
      "<div class='c-image-container c-image-container--lazy' style='padding-bottom: 66.66666666666666%'>",
      "  <div class='c-image-container--lazy__wrapper'>",
      "    <img class='c-image' loading='lazy'",
      "      src='", image.path, "'",
      "      alt='", image.alt, "'>",
      "  </div>",
      "</div>"
    ].join("");
  }
  return template;
}

/**
 * Generate a template for the label
 * @param {String} label - the label text
 * @returns {String}
 */
function displayLabel(label) {
  var template = "";
  if (label === "opinion") {
    template = [
      "<div class='c-card__meta'>",
      "  <span class='c-card__label c-card__label--muted'>", label, "</span>",
      "</div>",
    ].join("");
  }
  return template;
}

/**
 * ************ API CALLS *****************
 */

/**
 * Get the personalized feed
 * @param {String} hashId - user's hash id
 * @param {String} env - environment
 * @returns {Promise<Object>}
 */
function getPerzonalizedTopics(hashId, env) {
  var url = "https://myglobe-" + env + ".theglobeandmail.com/v1/user/personalizedarticles";
  var postBody = {
    "hashId": hashId
  };
  var config = {
    method: "POST",
    mode: "cors",
    headers: {
      "Content-Type": "application/json"
    },
    body: JSON.stringify(postBody)
  };

  return fetch(url, config)
    .then(function fn(res) {
      if (res.status !== 200) {
        throw "[ARC-6292] fetch error for personalized endpoint" + url;
      }
      return res.json();
    })
    .then(function fn(data) {
      return data;
    })
    .catch(function efn(err) {
      console.error("[ARC-6292] fetch error for personalized endpoint: " + err);
    });
}

/**
 * Follow or unfollow the topic
 * @param {String} action - "follow" or "unfollow"
 * @param {String} topic - topic name
 * @param {Boolean} isFollowingAuthor - true is following author button
 * @returns {Promise<Object>}
 */
function followUnfollowTopic(action, topic, isFollowingAuthor) {
  var path = isFollowingAuthor ? "author/" : "topic/";
  var env = getEnv();
  var hashId = getUserGuid();
  var url = "https://myglobe-" + env + ".theglobeandmail.com/v1/user/" + path + action;
  var postBody = {
    "hashId": hashId,
    "topicSlug": topic
  };
  var config = {
    method: "POST",
    mode: "cors",
    headers: {
      "Content-Type": "application/json"
    },
    body: JSON.stringify(postBody)
  };

  return fetch(url, config)
    .then(function fn(res) {
      if (res.status !== 200) {
        throw "Error following or unfollowing the topic: " + url;
      }
      return res.json();
    })
    .then(function fn(data) {
      return data;
    })
    .catch(function efn(err) {
      console.error("[ARC-6292] fetch error for follow/unfollow endpoint: " + err);
    });
}

// ************** FOLLOWING FUNCTIONALITY *****************
/**
 * Attach event listeners to following icons/buttons
 */
function addFollowingFunctionality() {
  var btns = qsa(".darwin-personalized-feed__topics .c-topic-button");
  if (!btns.length) {
    return;
  }
  btns.forEach(function fn(btn) {
    btn.addEventListener("mouseover", function fn() {
      btn.classList.remove("js-topic-clicked");
      buttonToggle(btn, "over");
    });

    btn.addEventListener("mouseout", function fn() {
      buttonToggle(btn, "out");
    });

    btn.addEventListener("click", function fn() {
      updateFollowUnfollowStatus(btn);
      btn.classList.add("js-topic-clicked");
    });
  });
}

/**
 * Follow or unfollow a topic
 * @param {HTMLElement} el - button element
 */
function updateFollowUnfollowStatus(el) {
  var status = el.getAttribute("data-status");
  var topicSlug = el.getAttribute("data-slug");
  var topicName = el.getAttribute("data-topic");
  var isFollowingAuthor = el.dataset.topicType === "author";
  var topicType = isFollowingAuthor ? "author" : "topic";
  var action = status === "following" ? "unfollow" : "follow";

  followUnfollowTopic(action, topicSlug, isFollowingAuthor)
    .then(function fn(res) {
      console.log("[ARC-6292] fetch success: ", res);
      var setStatus = "following";
      var text = "following";
      var ariaLabelText = "Unfollow this " + topicType + ": " + topicName;
      if (status === "following") {
        setStatus = "unfollowing";
        text = "Follow";
        ariaLabelText = "Follow this " + topicType + ": " + topicName;
      }
      analyticsLayer.push({
        "event": "clickEvent",
        "clickEvent": {
          "type": "button",
          "feature": isFollowingAuthor ? "author" : "topic",
          "label": topicName.toLowerCase(),
          "action": action
        }
      });

      el.dataset.status = setStatus;
      el.setAttribute("aria-label", ariaLabelText);
      qs(".c-button__text", el).innerText = text;
    });
}

/**
 * Update icon state on mouseover/mouseout
 * @param {HTMLElement} el - button element
 * @param {String} action - either "out" or "over"
 */
function buttonToggle(el, action) {
  var status = el.getAttribute("data-status");
  var text = "Follow";
  var hoverText = "Follow";
  if (status === "following") {
    text = "Following";
    hoverText = "Unfollow";
  }

  if (action === "out" && !el.classList.contains("js-topic-clicked")) {
    qs(".c-button__text", el).innerText = text;
  } else if (action === "out" && el.classList.contains("js-topic-clicked") && status === "unfollowing") {
    qs(".c-button__text", el).innerText = "Follow";
  } else if (action === "over") {
    qs(".c-button__text", el).innerText = hoverText;
  }
}

    "      <span class='c-button__text'>View following page</span>",
    "    </a>",
    "  </div>",
    "</div>"
  ].join("");
}

/**
 * Display "Follow", "Following" buttons
 * @param {Object} tData
 * @returns {String}
 */
function displayFollowingButton(tData) {
  var topicName = tData.topicName;
  var topicSlug = tData.topicSlug;
  var topicType = tData.topicType;
  var topicImg = tData.topicImg;
  var isAuthor = topicType === "author";
  var authorImg = isAuthor && topicImg
    ? "<img class='c-topic-author-photo' src='" + topicImg + "' alt='" + topicName + "'>"
    : "";
  var template = isAuthor ? "/authors/" : "/topics/";
  var href = window.tgam.env.baseRootAbsoluteUrl + template + topicSlug;
  var linkClasses = isAuthor ? "c-topic-link c-topic-link--author" : "c-topic-link";
  return [
    "  <div class='c-topic-group__body'>",
    "      <div class='c-topic-group__items'>",
    "      <div class='c-topic'>",
    "        <a href='", href, "' class='", linkClasses, "'>", authorImg, topicName, "</a>",
    "        <button class='c-button c-button--white-primary c-button--small c-topic-button' data-status='unfollowing' type='button' aria-label='Follow this topic: ", topicName, "' data-slug='", topicSlug, "' data-topic-type='", topicType, "' data-topic='", topicName, "'>",
    "          <span class='c-button__text'> Follow </span>",
    "        </button>",
    "      </div>",
    "      </div>",
    "  </div>",
  ].join("");
}

/**
 * Display topic list - used by both Recommended and Trending topics
 * @param {Array} topics - list of topics
 * @param {String} topicsType - 'rec' or 'trend'
 * @returns {String}
 */
function displayTopicList(topics, topicsType) {
  var topicList = topics.map(displayTopic).join("");
  var heading = topicsType === "trend" ? "Trending topics" : "Consider following";
  var header = ["<h3 class='c-topic-group__heading'>", heading, "</h3>"].join("");
  var displayHeading = topics.length > 0 ? header : "";
  return [
    "<div class='c-topic-group'>",
    displayHeading,
    "  <div class='c-topic-group__body'>",
    "    <ul class='c-topic-group__items'>", topicList, "</ul>",
    "  </div>",
    "</div>"
  ].join("");
}

/**
 * Display one topic (with a link and following button)
 * @param {Object} topic
 * @returns {String}
 */
function displayTopic(topic) {
  var topicName = topic.name;
  var topicSlug = topic.slug;
  var topicType = topic.authorTopic ? "author" : "topic";
  var folowingStatus = "unfollowing";
  var template = topic.authorTopic ? "/authors/" : "/topics/";
  var href = window.tgam.env.baseRootAbsoluteUrl + template + topicSlug;
  var ariaText = "Follow";
  if (topic.following) {
    folowingStatus = "following";
    ariaText = "Unfollow";
  }
  var btnText = ariaText;
  var img = topic.authorTopic && topic.authorMetadata && topic.authorMetadata.image ? topic.authorMetadata.image : "";
  var authorImg = img ? "<img class='c-topic-author-photo' src='" + img + "' alt='" + topic.name + "'>" : "";
  var linkClasses = topic.authorTopic ? "c-topic-link c-topic-link--author" : "c-topic-link";

  return [
    "<li class='c-topic'>",
    "  <a href='", href, "' class='", linkClasses, "'>", authorImg, topicName, "</a>",
    "  <button class='c-button c-button--white-primary c-button--small c-topic-button' data-status='", folowingStatus, "' data-slug='", topicSlug, "' data-topic='", topicName, "' data-topic-type='", topicType, "' type='button' aria-label='", ariaText, " this ", topicType, ": ", topicName, "'>",
    "    <span class='c-button__text'>", btnText, "</span>",
    "  </button>",
    "</li>"
  ].join("");
}

/**
 * Display three topics with one story for every topic.
 * Intended for users that follow 0 topics.
 * Either three trending or recommended topics will be displayed.
 * @param {Array} topics
 * @param {String} topicVariation - "rec" or "trend"
 * @returns {String}
 */
function displayTrenRecomTopicsAndStory(topics, topicVariation) {
  var uniqueStories = generateUniqueStory(topics);
  var stories = uniqueStories.map(function fn(topic) {
    // API sends 3 stories per topic, but we need to display only 1 story per topic
    // In very rare cases after deduping (see generateUniqueStory()) there may be no stories left to display (as they're already on the page)
    // In that case - drop the topic
    if (!topic.items.length) {
      return;
    }
    // Grab one article
    var article = topic.items[0];
    var topicSlug = topic.slug;
    var topicName = topic.name;
    var topicType = topic.type;
    var topicImg = topic.img;
    var topicData = {
      topicSlug: topicSlug,
      topicName: topicName,
      topicType: topicType,
      topicVariation: topicVariation,
      topicImg: topicImg
    };
    return displayCard(article, topicData);
  }).join("");

  var href = window.tgam.env.baseRootAbsoluteUrl + "/your-globe/#following";
  var headline = topicVariation === "trend" ? "Trending topics to follow" : "Recommended for you";

  return [
    "<div class='darwin-personalized-feed__cards'>",
    "  <div class='darwin-personalized-feed__cards-label'>", headline, "</div>",
    stories,
    "  <div class='darwin-personalized-feed__topics-footer'>Visit your <a class='darwin-personalized-feed__topics-visit-feed darwin-personalized-feed-link ' href='", href, "'>Following</a> page to view more of your personal feed.</div>",
    "</div>"
  ].join("");
}

/**
 * Display latest stories (max 5)
 * @param {Array} articles
 * @returns {String}
 */
function displayLatestMarkup(articles) {
  var topicType = "latest";
  var stories = articles.map(function fn(a) {
    var topicData = {
      topicSlug: null,
      topicName: null,
      topicType: topicType
    };
    return displayCard(a, topicData);
  }).join("");
  var href = window.tgam.env.baseRootAbsoluteUrl + "/your-globe/#following";
  var storiesNum = articles.length;
  var message = "View more stories in your Following feed";
  if (storiesNum < 5) {
    message = "Visit earlier stories in your Following feed";
  }
  return [
    "<div class='darwin-personalized-feed__cards'>",
    "  <div class='darwin-personalized-feed__topics__latest-label'> The latest in topics and authors you follow</div>", stories,
    "  <div class='darwin-personalized-feed__topics-footer'><a class='darwin-personalized-feed__topics__earlier-label' href='", href, "'>", message, "</a></div>",
    "</div>"
  ].join("");
}

/**
 * Generates story card markup
 * @param {Object} article - to display
 * @param {Object} topicData (topicName, topicSlug, topicType)
 * @returns {String}
 */
function displayCard(article, topicData) {
  var tSlug = topicData.topicSlug;
  var tName = topicData.topicName;
  var tVariation = topicData.topicVariation;
  var followingTopic;
  var timeTemplate;
  var analyticsModifier = "topic: ";
  if (tSlug && tName) {
    // We are displaying topic name and one story card
    followingTopic = displayFollowingButton(topicData);
    timeTemplate = displayDateTag(article);
  } else {
    // We are displaying latest card
    // Stories in latest feed can be either from following an author or topic
    // If it's an author there is no topics property (only authors)
    var topic = article.topics ? article.topics[0] : article.authors[0];
    tName = article.authors ? topic.byline : topic.name;
    analyticsModifier = !article.topics ? "author: " : "topic: ";
    tSlug = topic.slug;
  }
  var label = getLabel(article);
  var image = getImage(article, label);
  var labelTemplate = displayLabel(label);
  var imageTemplate = displayImage(image);
  var headline = article.headlines.basic;
  var href = window.tgam.env.baseUrl + article.canonical_url;
  var sophiId = article._id;
  var version = tVariation === "rec" ? "recommended" : "trending";
  if (tVariation === "latest") {
    version = "following";
  }
  var dataAnalyticsClick = JSON.stringify({
    type: "link",
    feature: "following feed",
    contentId: sophiId,
    label: analyticsModifier + tName.toLowerCase() + ": " + headline.toLowerCase(),
    page: "sec:homepage:personalized feed:" + version,
    hierarchy: 1
  });

  var cardMarkup = "";
  if (!topicData.topicSlug && !topicData.topicName) {
    cardMarkup = [
      "<a class='c-card__grid c-card__link'",
      "  data-sophi='", sophiId, "'",
      "  data-analyticsclick='", dataAnalyticsClick, "'",
      "  href='", href, "' >",
      "  <div class='c-card__content'>",
      "    <div class='c-card__topics'>",
      "      <span class='c-card__topics__item'>", tName, "</span>",
      "    </div>",
      "    <div class='c-card__hed'>",
      "      <span class='c-card__hed-text'>", headline, "</span>",
      "    </div>",
      labelTemplate,
      "  </div>",
      "  <div class='c-card__media'>", imageTemplate, "</div>",
      "</a>"
    ].join("");
  } else {
    cardMarkup = [
      "    <div class='c-card__topics'>",
      followingTopic,
      "    </div>",
      "    <a class='c-card__grid c-card__link'",
      "      data-sophi='", sophiId, "'",
      "      data-analyticsclick='", dataAnalyticsClick, "'",
      "      href='", href, "'>",
      "      <div class='c-card__content'>",
      "        <div class='c-card__hed'>",
      "          <span class='c-card__hed-text'>", headline, "</span>",
      "        </div>",
      "        <span class='c-card__meta'>", timeTemplate, "</span>",
      "      </div>",
      "      <div class='c-card__media'>", imageTemplate, "</div>",
      "    </a>",
    ].join("");
  }
  return [
    "  <div class='c-card c-card--following c-card--latest'>",
    cardMarkup,
    "  </div>",
  ].join("");
}

/**
 * Displays three recommended or trending topics with a story
 * @param {Array} topicsAndStory - list of topics with one story
 * @param {String} topicVariation - either "rec" or "trend"
 */
function noFollowingDisplayRecommended(topicsAndStory, topicVariation) {
  //console.log("[ARC-6292] Three topics and one story: " + JSON.stringify(topicsAndStory));
  var topicLists = displayTrenRecomTopicsAndStory(topicsAndStory, topicVariation);
  var header = displayFollowingInstructions();

  var markup = [
    "<div class='darwin-personalized-feed__intro'>", header, "</div>",
    topicLists,
    " </div>"
  ].join("");
  displayPersonalizedFeed(markup);
}

/**
 * Display a group of recommended topics when a user doesn't have any latest stories
 * @param {Array} topics - a list of recommended or trending topics
 * @param {String} variation - either 'rec' or 'trend'
 */
function displayRecommendedTopicsNoLatest(topics, variation) {
  var header = getContainerHeader();
  var topicsList = displayTopicList(topics, variation);
  var markup = [
    "<div class='darwin-personalized-feed__intro'>", header, "</div>",
    "<p class='darwin-personalized-feed__uptodate'>",
    "  You're up to date on your Following feed. Check again later for new stories.",
    "</p>",
    topicsList,
    " </div>"
  ].join("");

  displayPersonalizedFeed(markup);
}

/**
 * Displays a list of latest stories (max 5) and recommended topics
 * @param {Array} articles - array of latest articles
 * @param {Array} recommended - list of recommended topics
 */
function displayLatestAndRecommended(articles, recommended) {
  var latestArticles = displayLatestMarkup(articles);
  var header = getContainerHeader();
  var recomendedTopics = recommended.length > 0 ? displayTopicList(recommended) : "";
  var markup = [
    "<div class='darwin-personalized-feed__intro'>", header, "</div>",
    latestArticles,
    recomendedTopics,
    " </div>"
  ].join("");

  displayPersonalizedFeed(markup);
}

/**
 * Display personalized feed for all cases
 * @param {String} html - content of personalized feed
 */
function displayPersonalizedFeed(html) {
  var packageStoryList = qsa(".c-package--story-list--cards.l-full-contained");
  if (!packageStoryList.length) {
    return;
  }
  var inTheKnow = packageStoryList.pop();

  var inTheKnowLabel = qs(".c-package__label", inTheKnow);
  inTheKnow.classList.remove("l-full-contained");
  inTheKnowLabel.classList.remove("c-package__label");
  inTheKnowLabel.classList.add("c-section-title");
  inTheKnowLabel.innerText = "In the Know";
  var inTheKnowMarkup = inTheKnow.outerHTML;
  var parent = inTheKnow.closest(".l-full-width");

  parent.innerHTML = [
    "<div class='l-full-contained darwin-personalized-feed__container'>",
    "  <div class='darwin-personalized-feed__topics'>",
    html,
    "  <div class='darwin-personalized-feed__intheknow'>", inTheKnowMarkup, "</div>",
    "</div>"
  ].join("");

  addFollowingFunctionality();
}

// * ************ HELPER FUNCTIONS TO BUILD THE MARKUP *****************
/**
 * Remove duplicate articles
 * @param {Array} originalArr - list of articles
 * @returns {Array} - of articles
 */
function removeDuplicateArticles(originalArr) {
  var allArticlesHomepage = qsa("[data-sophi]").map(function fn(article) {
    return article.dataset.sophi;
  });
  var uniqueArticles = originalArr.filter(function fn(article) {
    return allArticlesHomepage.indexOf(article._id) == -1;
  });
  return uniqueArticles;
}

/**
 * Build recommended topic list (topics and authors)
 * Also include topic type in every topic array
 * @param {Object} rec - { recommendedTopics: [], recommendedAuthors: []}
 * @returns {Array} of topics to display
 */
function generateTopicsAndAuthorsList(rec) {
  var recommendedTopics = rec.recommendedTopics || [];
  var recommendedAuthors = rec.recommendedAuthors || [];
  return recommendedAuthors.concat(recommendedTopics);
}

/**
 * Generate latest stories after some filtering
 * @param {Array} latest - array of days
 * @returns {Array} of filtered articles
 */
function generateLatestStories(latest) {
  var articles = [];
  // Latest is an array of days, so we need to create a new array of stories from last three days
  var articles = latest.reduce(function fn(result, item) {
    return result.concat(item.items);
  }, []);
  // Remove articles that are already on the homepage
  var uniqueArticles = removeDuplicateArticles(articles);

  //console.log("[ARC-6292] Array of latest stories: " + JSON.stringify(articles));
  //console.log("[ARC-6292] Array of latest stories after deduping: " + JSON.stringify(uniqueArticles));

  // After all filtering we need to display only five latest articles to the user
  var articlesToDisplay = uniqueArticles.slice(0, 5);

  return articlesToDisplay;
}

/**
 * For every topic - generate one unique story
 * @param {Array} topics - array of topics (with five stories for every topic)
 * @returns {Array} - array of topics with one unique story
 */
function generateUniqueStory(topics) {
  var uniqueArticles = topics.map(function fn(t) {
    var uniqueItems = removeDuplicateArticles(t.items);
    return {
      topicId: t.topicId,
      name: t.name,
      slug: t.slug,
      type: t.authorTopic ? "author" : "topic",
      img: t.authorTopic ? t.authorMetadata.image : "",
      items: uniqueItems.slice(0, 1) // only one story is needed
    };
  });
  return uniqueArticles;
}

/**
 * Call the personalized API to display topics to the user
 * @param {Object} data - topics data
 */
function startTest(data) {
  var totalTopicsFollowed = data.totalTopicsFollowed || 0;
  var totalAuthorsFollowed = data.totalAuthorsFollowed || 0;
  var recommendedTopics = data.recommendedTopics || [];
  var recommendedAuthors = data.recommendedAuthors || [];
  var latestStories = data.articles || [];
  var topics = recommendedTopics.length > 0 || recommendedAuthors.length > 0 ? generateTopicsAndAuthorsList(data) : [];
  if (totalTopicsFollowed > 0 || totalAuthorsFollowed > 0) {
    // Display user's latest feed and recommended topic list
    if (latestStories.length === 0) {
      // No latest stories, display recommended topic list only (or trending if no recommended topics)
      var variation = "rec";
      if (topics.length === 0) { // there are recommended topics
        topics = data.trendingTopics || [];
        variation = "trend";
      }
      displayRecommendedTopicsNoLatest(topics, variation);
    } else {
      // There are latest stories
      var articlesToDisplay = generateLatestStories(latestStories);
      if (articlesToDisplay.length > 0) {
        displayLatestAndRecommended(articlesToDisplay, topics);
      } else {
        // After deduping no latest stories are left
        displayRecommendedTopicsNoLatest(topics, variation);
      }
    }
  } else {
    // User doesn't follow any topics, show recommended and one story for each topic
    var topicVariation = "rec";
    var topics = recommendedAuthors.concat(recommendedTopics) || [];
    if (topics.length === 0) {
      // There are no recommended topics for this user, show trending topics
      topicVariation = "trend";
      topics = data.trendingTopics || [];
    }
    noFollowingDisplayRecommended(topics, topicVariation);
  }
}

/**
 * 3...2...1..START
 */

  console.log("[ARC-6292] init");
  var testIsEnabled = /token=arc6292/.test(window.location.search);
  console.log("[ARC-6292] testIsEnabled: ", testIsEnabled);
  var testGroup = userTestGroup();
  if (testGroup === "variant" || testIsEnabled) {
    setUnitState("arc6292", "variant");
    console.log("[ARC-6292] test group: variant");

      return;
    }
    var base = getEnv();
    getPerzonalizedTopics(hashId, base)
      .then(startTest);
  }
  if (testGroup === "control") {
    console.log("[ARC-6292] test group: control");
    setUnitState("arc6292", "control");
  }
}
